    /*******************TABS SLIDER HOME PAGE*********/
   var refreshIntervalId;
	jQuery(window).load(function() {
		refreshIntervalId	= setInterval(autoSlide,7000);
	});
	/*Trigger next tab of slider */
	function autoSlide()
	{
		if(jQuery("body.home .extra_tabs").length)
		{
			let totalIndex		= jQuery(".extra_tabs ul.tabs-nav li").length;
			let activeIndex 	= jQuery(".extra_tabs ul.tabs-nav li").index(jQuery('li.tab-item-active')[0]);
			let nextActiveIndex	= activeIndex+1;
			if(totalIndex<=nextActiveIndex)
			{
				nextActiveIndex=0;
			}		
			jQuery(".extra_tabs ul.tabs-nav li").eq(nextActiveIndex).find("a").trigger("click");
		}
	}
	jQuery(".extra_tabs ul.tabs-nav li a").on("click",function(){
		clearInterval(refreshIntervalId);
		refreshIntervalId	= setInterval(autoSlide,7000);
	});

  if (jQuery(window).width() > 993)
    {
		  var heights = jQuery('html[lang="es-ES"] footer .col-footer-menus .footer-menu.footer-menu--regular-menu:first-child').map(function ()
		{
			var height_max = jQuery(this).height();

		}).get();
